itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"https://schema.org/Article\">\n        <div class=\"td-post-header\">\n\n            <ul class=\"td-category\"><li class=\"entry-category\"><a class=\"td-post-title\">\n                <h1 class=\"entry-title\">How to Register you SimCard Details Using Your National ID With Your Phone</h1>\n\n                \n\n                <div class=\"td-module-meta-info\">\n                    <div class=\"td-post-author-name\">By <a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/author/onathan/\">Nathan Ernest Olupot</a> - </div>                    <div class=\"td-post-date\"><time class=\"entry-date updated td-module-date\" datetime=\"2017-04-12T17:21:23+00:00\">April 12, 2017</time></div>                    <div class=\"td-post-comments\"><a <div class=\"td-post-content\">\n\n        \n        <p>Following a directive from the Government regulatory body of communications in Uganda; <a href=\"http://ucc.co.ug\" target=\"_blank\">Uganda Communication Commission</a> (UCC) on Tuesday this week issued a <a href=\"http://pctechmag.com/2017/04/ugandans-given-7-days-to-update-their-simcard-registration-details-before-deactivation/\" target=\"_blank\">7 day ultimatum to all Ugandans to have their SimCard registration</a> particulars updated using their National IDs or Passports, short of which they would be deactivated, if not taken serious or done in time.</p>\n\n <!-- A generated by theme --> \n\n<script async=\"\" src=\"//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js\"></script><div class=\"td-g-rec td-g-rec-id-content_inlineleft\">\n<script type=\"text/javascript\">\nvar td_screen_width = document.body.clientWidth;\n\n                    if ( td_screen_width >= 1140 ) {\n                (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});\n                    }\n                \n                    if ( td_screen_width < 768 ) {\n                        /* Phones */\n style=\"display:inline-block;width:200px;height:200px\" data-ad-client=\"ca-pub-1387343816437996\" data-ad-slot=\"9891713214\" data-adsbygoogle-status=\"done\"><ins id=\"aswift_2_expand\" style=\"display:inline-table;border:none;height:200px;margin:0;padding:0;position:relative;visibility:visible;width:200px;background-color:transparent\"><ins id=\"aswift_2_anchor\" if(h.match){try{h=s.upd(h,i)}catch(e){}w.location.replace(h)}}\" id=\"aswift_2\" name=\"aswift_2\" style=\"left:0;position:absolute;top:0;\"></iframe></ins></ins></ins>\n</div>\n\n <!-- end A --> \n\n<p>The deadline for this process is Wednesday April 12th, 2017. This directive affects both our new and existing customers.</p>\n<p><em>“All existing subscribers should present their National ID’s to their operators for verification within 7 days,” <a href=\"https://twitter.com/UCC_Official/status/851735668883685376?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw&amp;ref_url=http%3A%2F%2Fpctechmag.com%2F2017%2F04%2Fugandans-given-7-days-to-update-their-simcard-registration-details-before-deactivation%2F\" target=\"_blank\">UCC writes in a tweet</a>.</em></p>\n<p>To avoid disconnection or disturbance or any other problems, in just a few simple steps, have you SimCard details updated by you. The good news is that you won’t have to go&nbsp;line up at at the telecom outlets&nbsp;for this. If you see it’s impossible/might be difficult for you, ask a friend to help you out.</p>\n<p>The acceptable customer identification documents for SIM registration are:</p>\n<ol>\n<ol>\n<ol>\n<li>Ugandans- National identification card.</li>\n<li>Non-Ugandans- Passport.</li>\n<li>Refugees- Registration documents from office of the Prime Minister.</li>\n<li>Corporate bodies- Registration documents certified by the Uganda Registration Services.</li>\n</ol>\n</ol>\n</ol>\n<p>In this scenario, we used a National ID!</p>\n<p>So follow these&nbsp;four simple steps and in less than a minute or two, you will be done. We tried this on MTN and Airtel, but the process is still the same.</p>\n<p><strong>Step One:</strong> Launch you dial app, and dial *197# and press the send button or call button. If you’re phone is a dual SimCard holder, select one operator at a time. For instance if you’ve MTN and Airtel, you can choose which to start with, in this example we started with MTN (then followed the same steps for Airtel).</p>\n<div id=\"gallery-1\" class=\"gallery galleryid-45826 gallery-columns-2 gallery-size-medium\"><figure class=\"gallery-item\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"gallery-icon portrait\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-6.png\"><img width=\"169\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-6-169x300.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-6-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-6-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-6.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 169px) 100vw, 169px\"></a>\n\t\t\t</div></figure><figure class=\"gallery-item\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"gallery-icon portrait\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-7.png\"><img width=\"169\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-7-169x300.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-7-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-7-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-7.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 169px) 100vw, 169px\"></a>\n\t\t\t</div></figure>\n\t\t</div>\n\n<p><strong>Step Two:</strong> From the pop-up option, select the option of <strong>National ID Details</strong>. When we carried out this, we found out that MTN had three options on the pop-up list and Airtel had only two. But don’t worry, just select the ‘National ID Details’ option, and click OK or send.</p>\n<div id=\"gallery-2\" class=\"gallery galleryid-45826 gallery-columns-2 gallery-size-medium\"><figure class=\"gallery-item\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"gallery-icon portrait\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-8.png\"><img width=\"169\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-8-169x300.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium\" alt=\"\" aria-describedby=\"gallery-2-45834\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-8-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-8-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-8.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 169px) 100vw, 169px\"></a>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<figcaption class=\"wp-caption-text gallery-caption\" id=\"gallery-2-45834\">\n\t\t\t\tMTN\n\t\t\t\t</figcaption></figure><figure class=\"gallery-item\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"gallery-icon portrait\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-9.png\"><img width=\"169\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-9-169x300.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium\" alt=\"\" aria-describedby=\"gallery-2-45835\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-9-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-9-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-9.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 169px) 100vw, 169px\"></a>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<figcaption class=\"wp-caption-text gallery-caption\" id=\"gallery-2-45835\">\n\t\t\t\tAirtel\n\t\t\t\t</figcaption></figure>\n\t\t</div>\n\n<p><strong>Step Three:</strong> You will be asked to enter your National ID Number (NIN).&nbsp;Your&nbsp;NIN is the&nbsp;13 digit number on your ID that starts with either <strong>CF or CM (CM*******)</strong>. To locate the NIN, its just below the Nationality section or above the Date of Birth section.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-3.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-45836\" src=\"http://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"250\" height=\"445\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-3.png 480w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-3-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-3-236x420.png 236w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 250px) 100vw, 250px\"></a></p>\n<p><strong>Step Four:</strong> You’re asked to enter you’re details, this is your First Name and Surname. With MTN, you’re asked to enter you’re First Name first and then Surname follows (This is vice-versa to Airtel, ‘but still its the same procedure’.).</p>\n<div id=\"gallery-3\" class=\"gallery galleryid-45826 gallery-columns-2 gallery-size-medium\"><figure class=\"gallery-item\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"gallery-icon portrait\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-4.png\"><img width=\"169\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-4-169x300.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-4-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-4-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-4.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 169px) 100vw, 169px\"></a>\n\t\t\t</div></figure><figure class=\"gallery-item\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"gallery-icon portrait\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-10.png\"><img width=\"169\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-10-169x300.png\" class=\"attachment-medium size-medium\" alt=\"\" aria-describedby=\"gallery-3-45838\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-10-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-10-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-10.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 169px) 100vw, 169px\"></a>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<figcaption class=\"wp-caption-text gallery-caption\" id=\"gallery-3-45838\">\n\t\t\t\tFirst Name\n\t\t\t\t</figcaption></figure>\n\t\t</div>\n\n<p><strong>Step Five:</strong> You will receive a confirmation that states “<em>Your SIM is fully registered, Thank You.”</em> or <em>“Dear customer, your request has been accepted successfully”</em> for Airtel and MTN respectively.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-5.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-45839\" src=\"http://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-5-169x300.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"250\" height=\"445\" srcset=\"https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-5-169x300.png 169w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-5-236x420.png 236w, https://pctechmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/SimCard-Reg-with-NIN-5.png 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 250px) 100vw, 250px\"></a></p>\n<p>As per the UCC directive, all SIM cards whose details are not updated by <strong>Thursday April 20th, 2017</strong> shall be deactivated.</p>\n<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><strong>Editor’s Note:</strong></span> If you read this article, inform a friend to tell a friend, and a friend. Don’t get disconnected.</p><div class=\"related-posts\">\n<div id=\"related-posts-post\" class=\"related-posts-type\">\n<h4>See Also:</h4>\n<ul>\n<li><a
